<script type="text/javascript" src="/portamento-min.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript" src="/jquery.autocomplete.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">

	var MAX_COMPARE = 5;

	$(document).ready( function( $) {
		// Floating sidebar
	  $('#sidebar').portamento();

	});

	$(document).on('keydown.autocomplete', '#autocomplete', function() {
		jQuery(this).autocomplete({
			//lookup: lookupCPUs,
			serviceUrl: '/autocomplete/cpu/',
			onSelect: function(suggestion){
				myCmp.addCPU( suggestion.data, suggestion.value, 1 );
			},
			width: 300,
			minChars: 2
		});
	});

	$("#sidebar_minimize, #sidebar_restore").click( function(event) {
		event.preventDefault();
		jQuery('#portamento_container').toggle(	);
		jQuery('#sb_restore').toggle();
	});

	var myCmp = ( function() {
		var pub = {};

		// Private

		var CPUs = [];

		pub.removeAll = function()
		{
			CPUs.length = 0;
			jQuery.post( "/compareAjax.php", { action: "removeAll"} );
			updateSidebar();
		};

		pub.addCPU = function( CPUId, CPUName, CPUCount  )
		{
			CPUCount = typeof CPUCount !== 'undefined' ? CPUCount : 1;

			for( var i = 0; i < CPUs.length; i++ )
				if( CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId == CPUId && CPUs[i].cpuCount == CPUCount )
						return; // Already added

			if( CPUs.length < MAX_COMPARE )
			{
				CPUs.push( { "cpuDetailsId": CPUId, "name": CPUName, "cpuCount": CPUCount } );

				console.log ("Adding CPUId="+CPUId+"; CPUName="+CPUName+"; CPUCount="+CPUCount+" (Length="+CPUs.length+");");

				jQuery.post( "/compareAjax.php", { action: "add", cpuid: CPUId, cpuname: CPUName, cpucount: CPUCount}, function( data ) {
					console.log(data);
				});

				var indexcmp = document.getElementById('indexcmp');
				var indexcmp2 = document.getElementById('indexcmp2');
				var indexcmp3 = document.getElementById('indexcmp3');
				$("#indexcmp").empty();
				$("#indexcmp2").empty();
				$("#indexcmp3").empty();

				if( indexcmp )
					indexcmp.append(CPUs.length);
				if( indexcmp2 )
					indexcmp2.append(CPUs.length);
				if( indexcmp3 )
					indexcmp3.append(CPUs.length);

				updateSidebar();

			}
			else
			{
				//alert( "Maximum of " + MAX_COMPARE + " can be compared at one time." );
				var toast = document.getElementById("toast");
				var oldText = toast.innerHTML;
				var oldBgColor = toast.style.backgroundColor;
				var newMsg = "You can only compare " + MAX_COMPARE + " CPUs.";
				toast.innerHTML = '<div id="img"><svg viewBox="0 0 30 30"><use xlink:href="#icon-header-compare"></use></svg></div><div id="desc">' + newMsg + '</div>';
				toast.style.backgroundColor = "#AE0034";
    		launch_toast();
    		//toast.innerHTML = oldText;
    		//toast.style.backgroundColor = oldBgColor;
			}
		};

		// this function is an optimization that essentially does the following with one single AJAX call:
		// myCmp.removall();
		// myCmp.addCPU(...);
		// myCmp.addCPU(...);
		pub.setCPUvsCPU = function( CPUId1, CPUName1, CPUCount1, CPUId2, CPUName2, CPUCount2 , CPUId3=0, CPUName3=0, CPUCount3=0)
		{
			CPUCount1 = typeof CPUCount1 !== 'undefined' ? CPUCount1 : 1;
			CPUCount2 = typeof CPUCount2 !== 'undefined' ? CPUCount2 : 1;
			//CPUCount3 = typeof CPUCount3 !== 'undefined' ? CPUCount3 : 1;

			CPUs.length = 0;

			CPUs.push( { "cpuDetailsId": CPUId1, "name": CPUName1, "cpuCount": CPUCount1 } );
			console.log ("Adding CPUId="+CPUId1+"; CPUName="+CPUName1+"; CPUCount="+CPUCount1+" (Length="+CPUs.length+");");
			CPUs.push( { "cpuDetailsId": CPUId2, "name": CPUName2, "cpuCount": CPUCount2 } );
			console.log ("Adding CPUId="+CPUId2+"; CPUName="+CPUName2+"; CPUCount="+CPUCount2+" (Length="+CPUs.length+");");
			if (CPUCount3 > 0)
			{
				CPUs.push( { "cpuDetailsId": CPUId3, "name": CPUName3, "cpuCount": CPUCount3 } );
				console.log ("Adding CPUId="+CPUId3+"; CPUName="+CPUName3+"; CPUCount="+CPUCount3+" (Length="+CPUs.length+");");
			}

			jQuery.post( "/compareAjax.php", { action: "setversus",
				cpuid1: CPUId1, cpuname1: CPUName1, cpucount1: CPUCount1,
				cpuid2: CPUId2, cpuname2: CPUName2, cpucount2: CPUCount2,
				cpuid3: CPUId3, cpuname3: CPUName3, cpucount3: CPUCount3} );

			var indexcmp = document.getElementById('indexcmp');
			var indexcmp2 = document.getElementById('indexcmp2');
			var indexcmp3 = document.getElementById('indexcmp3');
			$("#indexcmp").empty();
			$("#indexcmp2").empty();
			$("#indexcmp3").empty();

			if( indexcmp )
				indexcmp.append(CPUs.length);
			if( indexcmp2 )
				indexcmp2.append(CPUs.length);
			if( indexcmp3 )
				indexcmp3.append(CPUs.length);

			updateSidebar();
		}

		pub.setCPUvsCPUArray = function( cpu_array )
		{
			console.log( "param: " + cpu_array );

			CPUs.length = 0;
			var i;
			for( i = 0; i < cpu_array.length; i++ )
			{
				CPUs.push( { "cpuDetailsId": cpu_array[i]['cpuid'], "name": cpu_array[i]['cpuname'], "cpuCount": (typeof cpu_array[i]['cpucount'] !== 'undefined' ? cpu_array[i]['cpucount'] : 1) } );
				console.log("Adding CPUId="+cpu_array[i]['cpuid']+"; CPUName="+cpu_array[i]['cpuname']+"; CPUCount="+cpu_array[i]['cpucount']+" (Length="+CPUs.length+");");
			}

			jQuery.post( "/compareAjax.php", { action: "setversusarray",
				'cpus': JSON.stringify(cpu_array) } )
								;

			var indexcmp = document.getElementById('indexcmp');
			var indexcmp2 = document.getElementById('indexcmp2');
			var indexcmp3 = document.getElementById('indexcmp3');
			$("#indexcmp").empty();
			$("#indexcmp2").empty();
			$("#indexcmp3").empty();

			if( indexcmp )
				indexcmp.append(CPUs.length);
			if( indexcmp2 )
				indexcmp2.append(CPUs.length);
			if( indexcmp3 )
				indexcmp3.append(CPUs.length);

			updateSidebar();

		}

		pub.removeCPU = function( CPUId, CPUCount )
		{
			CPUCount = typeof CPUCount !== 'undefined' ? CPUCount : 1;
			console.log( "Remove CPUId: " + CPUId + " CPUCount: " + CPUCount + "(Length:" + CPUs.length + ")");
			for( var i = 0; i < CPUs.length; i++ )
			{
				console.log ("i=" + i + "; CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId="+CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId+"; CPUs[i].cpuCount="+CPUs[i].cpuCount+";");
				if( CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId == CPUId && CPUs[i].cpuCount == CPUCount )
				{
					CPUs.splice( i, 1 );
					console.log("spliced i="+i+"; CPUId="+CPUId);
					jQuery.post( "/compareAjax.php", { action: "remove", cpuid: CPUId, cpucount: CPUCount } );
					var indexcmp = document.getElementById('indexcmp');
					var indexcmp2 = document.getElementById('indexcmp2');
					var indexcmp3 = document.getElementById('indexcmp3');
					$("#indexcmp").empty();
					$("#indexcmp2").empty();
					$("#indexcmp3").empty();
					if( indexcmp )
						indexcmp.append(CPUs.length);
					if( indexcmp2 )
						indexcmp2.append(CPUs.length);
					if( indexcmp3 )
						indexcmp3.append(CPUs.length);

					updateSidebar();

					break;
				}
			}
		};

		pub.compareCPUs = function( isButton )
		{
			if( CPUs.length < 2)
			{
				if (isButton)
					alert( "Please select more than " + CPUs.length + " CPU.");
				return;
			}

			var locationHref = "/compare";
			var paramString1 = "";
			var paramString2 = "";
			for( var i = 0; i < CPUs.length; i++ )
			{
				if( i )
				{
					paramString1 += " vs ";
					paramString2 += "vs";
				}

				var name = CPUs[i].name;
				var n = name.indexOf("@");
				if( n > 0 )
				{
					name = name.substr( 0, n-1 );
				}

				name = name.replace( /\//g, "", name );
				name = name.replace( /Intel\sCore\b/i, "Intel " );
				name = name.replace( /\s+/g, " ", name );

				paramString1 += name;
				paramString2 += "" + CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId;

				if( typeof CPUs[i].cpuCount !== 'undefined' )
				{
					if( Number.isInteger( CPUs[i].cpuCount ) && CPUs[i].cpuCount > 1 )
					{
						paramString2 += "." + CPUs[i].cpuCount.toString();
					}
				}
			}

			window.location.href = encodeURI(locationHref +
									"/" + paramString2 +
									"/" + paramString1.replace(/\s/g, "-"));
		}

		function updateSidebar()
		{
			console.log( "updateSideBar() Max Compare: " + MAX_COMPARE );

			var objSidebar = document.getElementById("sidebar");
			if( !objSidebar )
			{
				console.log( "Error: Object 'sidebar' not found!" );
				return;
			}

			var pSidebar = document.getElementById("sidebar_default_text");
			var tableSidebar = document.getElementById( "sidebar_table" );
			var buttonSidebar = document.getElementById( "sidebar_button" );
			var divTableSidebar = document.getElementById( "div_sidebar_table" );


			{

				pSidebar.style.display = (CPUs.length < 2) ? "block":"none";
				divTableSidebar.style.display = "block";
				buttonSidebar.style.display = "block";

				// Remove all previous rows
				while( tableSidebar.hasChildNodes() )
					tableSidebar.removeChild( tableSidebar.lastChild );

				// Header
				var header = tableSidebar.createTHead();
				var headRow = header.insertRow();

				var headCell = document.createElement("th");
				var col2 = headRow.insertCell();
				var col1 = headRow.insertCell();
				col1.setAttribute( "class", "ta-center" );
				col2.appendChild( document.createTextNode( "Compare List" ) );
				col1.appendChild( document.createTextNode( "" ) );
				// Create new rows for CPUs
				var body = tableSidebar.createTBody();
				for( var i = 0; i < CPUs.length; i++ )
				{

					var row = body.insertRow( -1 );
					row.setAttribute( "id", "" + CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId );

					if( i % 2 )
						row.setAttribute( "class", "alt" );

					var col2 = row.insertCell();
					col2.appendChild( document.createTextNode( "" + (i+1) + ": " + CPUs[i].name ));

					var col1 = row.insertCell( -1 );
					col1.setAttribute( "class", "ta-center" );
					var but = document.createElement( "button" );
					but.appendChild( document.createTextNode("X") );
					but.onclick = function(id, numCPUs) {
						return function(){

							pub.removeCPU( id, numCPUs );
							anim();

						};
					}(CPUs[i].cpuDetailsId, CPUs[i].cpuCount > 1 ? CPUs[i].cpuCount : 1);
					col1.appendChild( but );
				}

				if( i < MAX_COMPARE )
				{
					var row = body.insertRow( -1 );
					row.setAttribute( "id", "selectCPU" );

					if( i % 2 )
						row.setAttribute( "class", "alt" );

					var label = document.createElement( "label" );
					label.setAttribute("for", "autocomplete");
					label.setAttribute("style", "color: #00496B; font-size:10px;");
					label.appendChild( document.createTextNode("Add other CPU:") );
					var img = document.createElement( "img" );
					img.setAttribute("class", "icon-s-comp");
					img.setAttribute("src", "/img/compsearch.svg");
					var x = document.createElement( "input" );

					x.setAttribute( "id", "autocomplete" );
					x.setAttribute( "placeholder", "Intel Core ..." );
					x.setAttribute( "type", "text" );
					//x.setAttribute( "class", "input-box" );


					var col = row.insertCell();
					col.setAttribute( "colspan", 2 );
					col.appendChild( label );
					col.appendChild( document.createElement( "br" ));
					col.appendChild( img );
					col.appendChild( x );
				}
			}
		}

		$(document).ready( function( $) {
			updateSidebar()
		});
		return pub;
	}()	);

	function anim() {

		var indexcmp = document.getElementById('indexcmp');
			if(indexcmp.innerHTML < MAX_COMPARE) {
				$(".cmp-header a svg").addClass("anim-class");
				$(".cmp-header .number-cmp").addClass("anim-bounce-class");
				setTimeout(function () {
					$(".cmp-header a svg").removeClass('anim-class');
				}, 1500); }

	}

	function anim2() {

		$(".cmp-header a svg").addClass("anim-class");
		setTimeout(function () {
				$(".cmp-header a  svg").removeClass('anim-class');
		}, 1500);

	}

	function launch_toast(toastID) {
		//var indexcmp = document.getElementById("indexcmp");
    var toast = document.getElementById("toast");
    //toast.top = indexcmp.top+30;
    toast.className = "show";
    toast.style.display = "block";
    setTimeout(function(){ toast.className = toast.className.replace("show", ""); }, 5000);
	}
